            <p>This page allows you to specify the fields that can appear on the Campaign page. You can create up to 500 Campaign custom fields.</p>
            <p>Note that deleting a custom field will delete any filters that use the custom field. It may also change the result of Assignment or Escalation Rules that rely on the custom field data.</p>
